# Appendix — Architecture Read (manual analysis, code-only AST build)

> Analyst note: this build is **AST-only** (no LLM/semantic pass), so raw degree, god-node,
> and community-bridge metrics are inflated by large classes whose *own* members become graph
> mass. The verdicts below separate real architecture from these artifacts using the
> **ext% test**: the fraction of a node's neighbors that live in *other* files.
>
> - **ext% ≥ 70% + `imports`/`calls` dominant → real shared dependency (true hub).**
> - **ext% < 15% + `method` dominant → one monolithic class, not a hub (fat-class mirage).**

## God-node reality check (top 12 by degree)

| Class | Deg | ext% | Dominant edges | On-disk copies | Verdict |
|-------|----:|-----:|----------------|:--------------:|---------|
| `WarnaTable` | 2,526 | 100% | 1,259 imports + 1,264 calls | 5 | ✅ REAL shared util |
| `DlgCariPetugas` | 697 | 97% | 205 imports + 248 calls + 220 refs | 1 | ✅ REAL shared component |
| `frmUtama` | 1,310 | 2% | 1,280 `method` | 15 | ❌ Fat-class mirage |
| `akses` (×2 nodes) | 1,254 / 883 | 0% | ~1,250 `method` | 2 | ❌ Fat-class mirage (data bag) |
| `DlgReg` | 491 | 7% | 454 `method` | 1 | ❌ Fat-class mirage |
| `DlgKasirRalan` | 460 | 6% | 431 `method` | 1 | ❌ Fat-class mirage |
| `DlgRawatJalan` | 381 | 9% | 345 `method` | 1 | ❌ Fat-class mirage |
| `DlgKamarInap` | 378 | 7% | 349 `method` | 1 | ❌ Fat-class mirage |
| `DlgIGD` | 376 | 9% | 343 `method` | 1 | ❌ Fat-class mirage |
| `RMPenilaianAwalKeperawatanRanap…` | 326 | 8% | 300 `method` | 1 | ❌ Fat-class mirage |
| `DlgRawatInap` | 322 | 10% | 288 `method` | 1 | ❌ Fat-class mirage |

**Only 2 of the top 12 are genuine hubs:** `WarnaTable` (a 12-line JTable row-striping renderer
imported by 81% — 1,328/1,635 — of `src` forms) and `DlgCariPetugas` (staff-lookup dialog
referenced by ~200 forms). The rest are big classes whose degree measures *internal size*, not fan-in.

### Worked example: the `DlgResepObat` "bridge"
The report's top suggested question — why `DlgResepObat` bridges the drug-entry, PACS-imaging,
print, and drug-search communities — is **~80% artifact**. Of its 107 edges, 89 are internal.
The cross-community edges break down as:
- ✅ **Real dependency:** `DlgCariObat` / `DlgCariObat2` (drug-search dialogs it opens to pick meds).
- ⚠️ **Same class, split by clustering:** its own print methods (`ppLembarObat1/2`, `BtnPrint`) landed
  in the app-wide "Print Actions" community.
- ❌ **False bridge:** `.panggilPhoto()` (`DlgResepObat.java:2738`) was clustered into the Orthanc PACS
  community by name only — it actually renders a prescription-handover photo via an `<img>` to the
  hybrid web server (`bukti_penyerahan_resep_obat.photo`), with **no** DICOM/PACS involvement.

## (a) Fat-class refactor backlog

Ranked by file size; own-method counts from the graph. Highest-value decompositions first.

| Class | Lines | Own methods | Role |
|-------|------:|------------:|------|
| `src/simrskhanza/frmUtama.java` | 50,677 | 1,280 | Main menu — one handler per menu item |
| `src/simrskhanza/DlgKamarInap.java` | 21,388 | 349 | Inpatient room management |
| `src/simrskhanza/DlgReg.java` | 19,505 | 454 | Patient registration |
| `src/simrskhanza/DlgKasirRalan.java` | 18,834 | 431 | Outpatient cashier |
| `src/simrskhanza/DlgIGD.java` | 14,655 | 343 | Emergency (IGD) |
| `src/simrskhanza/DlgRawatJalan.java` | 14,615 | 345 | Outpatient care |
| `src/simrskhanza/DlgRawatInap.java` | 12,380 | 288 | Inpatient care |
| `src/simrskhanza/DlgPasien.java` | 10,150 | 214 | Patient master data |
| `src/fungsi/akses.java` | 5,187 | 1,250 | Permissions/session — a getter per DB column |
| `src/rekammedis/RMPenilaianAwalKeperawatan*` | — | 200–300 ea. | ~15 nursing-assessment forms |

`frmUtama.java` (**50,677 lines in one file**) is the standout. The `Dlg*` clinical dialogs
(10k–21k lines) mix UI layout, event handling, SQL, and business logic in a single class — the
highest-value splits. `akses` is not complex, just wide (1,250 trivial getters): treat as a
POJO/record extraction, not a decomposition.

## (b) Duplication map — no shared kernel across 23 sub-apps

**54 `src` classes are physically copied into other sub-apps.** Worst offenders:

| Copies | Class | What it is |
|-------:|-------|-----------|
| 18 | `koneksiDB.java` | DB connection factory |
| 15 | `sekuel.java` | SQL helper |
| 15 | `frmUtama.java` | The 50k-line main menu, duplicated 15× |
| 12 | `TextBox`, `TextArea`, `Table`, `ComboBox`, `Button`, `Label`, `Panel`, `CekBox`, `RadioButton`, `ScrollPane` | Custom Swing widget toolkit |
| 10 | `RunText*`, `panelisi*`, `panelGlass`, `Toolbar`, `Tanggal`, `ProgressBar`, `RoundedCornerBorder` | More shared widgets |

The `Khanza{Antrian*,HMS*}` desktop apps were each forked from a common base and carry their own
copies of the connection layer, SQL helper, and the entire custom widget set. There is no shared
library — a fix to `koneksiDB` or a widget must be applied in up to 18 places.

## Two structural problems + first step

1. **God classes** — `frmUtama` (50k lines) and the `Dlg*` clinical dialogs (10–21k) concentrate the
   whole app's logic in a handful of files. This is what inflates the god-node, surprising-connection,
   and community-bridge lists.
2. **No shared kernel** — infrastructure (`koneksiDB`, `sekuel`, the Swing widget set, `WarnaTable`,
   `akses`) is copy-pasted across 10–18 sub-apps.

**Highest-leverage first step:** extract `koneksiDB` + the custom widget toolkit + `WarnaTable` into
a single shared JAR that all 23 apps depend on. Then tackle `frmUtama` and the `Dlg*` dialogs.

_Appendix generated from the code-only AST graph (`graph.json`: 139,983 nodes · 353,122 edges) plus
on-disk verification (`grep`/`find`/`wc`). Metrics reflect structural extraction only._
